A Visit to the Belgenland

The Red Star Line's world cruise ship Belgenland, carrying 350 tourists, arrived at Sanjiaoshui outside Wusong at 6:30 PM the night before last and anchored overnight. The tourists disembarked in groups to sightsee on the night before last and yesterday morning. Yesterday, the reporter was invited to visit the ship, along with 20 other people. The passenger launch departed from the Customs Pier at 1:30 PM and, after an hour and a half, approached the Belgenland. After climbing the steps, we were led by a guide to visit the smoking room and the dining room. Then we went to the gymnasium and the swimming pool, which had a Japanese garden and a dance hall. Finally, we visited the ship's newly installed sound movie and wireless telephone. The captain hosted us with tea and snacks, and we returned at 7:00 PM. The ship was built in 1923, is 697 feet long and 79 feet wide, and has a tonnage of 27,200 tons. It is on its seventh world cruise. It left Shanghai last night at 9:00 PM, heading south.

Another Maritime Accident Involving Jianghai Vessels

▲Stranding丨Engine Damage丨Collision▲

▲Xinningxing Stranded The Sanbei Company's Changjiang liner Xinningxing was carrying a large number of goods for export from Shanghai to Lian. The draft reached 12 feet. When sailing to the Baihushan section of the river upstream, the water level was receding, with only 9 feet. Xinningxing could not pass through the area and the ship ran aground. The captain tried to reverse the ship, but it was ineffective. They immediately sent a radio distress call. The Shanghai Bureau received the message and ordered the Hankou branch to send four tugs to tow the ship. However, the bottom of the ship was stuck in the sand. After a day and night of towing, it was still not towed out. Yesterday, the bureau sent another telegram to Hankou, ordering the Hankou Bureau to send two shallow-water vessels, Yian and Yang'an, to the Baihushan section of the river to transfer the goods from the Xinningxing to the four tugs to reduce the draft by one foot and then try to tow the ship.

Qinghe Escapes Danger The Jardine Matheson Company's Chongqing vessel Qinghe ran aground in the Fujiang River on the 26th of last month while sailing upstream from Yichang. At that time, it was attacked by bandits, creating an extremely dangerous situation. Fortunately, the rescue vessel sent from Hankou arrived and the British soldiers on the rescue vessel repelled the river bandits. The cargo inside the ship was unloaded at the grounding site, and the vessel was finally freed. Yesterday, the company received a telegram from Hankou stating that although the Qinghe had escaped danger, the hull had been damaged by the grounding. It is now being sailed back to Shanghai to enter the dock for major repairs. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai in two or three days.

▲Jianguo Loses Blades The China Merchants Bureau's Jianguo vessel entered shallow water near Anqing. When the captain reversed the ship, two of the rear propeller blades were broken, and the ship lost its ability to sail. The Anhui Bureau sent two small vessels to tow it out. The Shanghai Bureau received the report and requested that the Weidedao send a tugboat to the Changjiang River to tow the Jianguo back to Shanghai. It is unloading cargo today and tomorrow and will enter the factory for repairs.

▲French Postal Ship Incident The French Postal Ship Company's Baodao S vessel collided with the Japanese Nisaki Shipping Company's Goshumaru in the Akashi Bay, Hyogo Prefecture, Japan. Yesterday, the Shanghai office received a telegram from the ship stating that it was to rescue the Japanese ship and that the ship was taking responsibility for the disaster, causing it to not be able to arrive as scheduled. The date must be delayed by 24 hours. Because the postal ship cannot postpone the export date, the company has decided to arrive in Shanghai tomorrow. It will only stay in Shanghai for one day and will depart for France on Saturday.

Zhejiang Sea Vessels Suspend Service

▲Tongyang Vessels Also Suspend Sailing

Six shipping companies operate on the coastal routes in eastern Zhejiang, such as Shanghai to Taizhou, Shipu, Zhoushan, Chuanshan, and other ports. Due to the end of the lunar year and a lack of cargo to load, the shipping companies decided yesterday to suspend service after the last vessel departs today, and to resume service on the third day of the lunar new year. In addition, the Shanghai Tongyang vessels have also decided to suspend sailing during the lunar new year under the pretext of repairing the vessels.

Mrs. Wright Departs for the Philippines

▲American Enthusiastic Anti-Drug Comrade

Mrs. Wright of the United States arrived in Shanghai last week after investigating the situation of opium and other drugs in the Philippines last month, to meet with anti-drug activists in Beijing and Shanghai to collect information on the various news of factory drunk products. She took the President Grant back to Manila yesterday morning. According to Mrs. Wright, she was the director of the American delegation to the Geneva International Opium Conference in 1925, and is now an important figure in the European anti-smoking work. She came to China for a very short period of time. It is said that she plans to come here again within two weeks to continue investigating everything. The anti-drug comrades in the city all believe that Mrs. Wright's trip to the Far East is of great importance, and the anti-smoking activists in Geneva also pay special attention to it. Mrs. Wright has written many books, all of which are famous in the world. She has been living since 1917, and after her husband, she has devoted herself to the anti-drug cause, because her husband was also a well-known anti-drug enthusiast in the East and West.

Central Bank Inspection Report

▲Eightieth Time

The Central Bank's Eightieth Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible notes by this bank. The eightieth inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on February 10, 1930. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: The total amount of convertible notes issued is 23,844,212 silver dollars, including 22,981,912 silver dollar notes and 862,300 supplementary coin notes (12 coppers). The total amount of convertible note reserve is 23,844,212 silver dollars, including a cash reserve of 20,452,772 silver dollars. This cash reserve includes 14,876,495.27 yuan stored in the bank's issuance vault, 2,006,917 yuan stored in branch banks in various ports, and 3,479,359.73 yuan stored in the industry (银业). The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 3,391,440 silver dollars. According to Article 3 of the Central Bank's Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. January 10, 1930, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisors (members) Gong Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jijing."

Court Order Explains Protest Certificate for Negotiable Instruments

The Shanghai Lawyers Association requested that the court clarify the procedure for making a protest certificate under Article 103 of the Negotiable Instruments Law, as the Negotiable Instruments Law and its implementation regulations did not mention it. The court forwarded this to the Department of Judicial Administration for interpretation and has now received an order from the Department. The order and official letter are recorded below: (1) The Jiangsu High Court Second Branch issued an order to comply with the matter. It received an instruction from the Department of Judicial Administration that the court had submitted a report requesting an interpretation of the procedure for a holder of a negotiable instrument to apply to the court for a protest certificate. The Department of Judicial Administration, after reviewing the report, submitted it to the Judicial Yuan for verification. The Judicial Yuan instructed that the holder's application to the court for a protest certificate should be considered a non-contentious matter, and fees should be collected in accordance with the Provisional Rules for Fee Collection for Non-Contentious Matters. The preparation of the certificate and all other matters may be handled by the court clerk. (2) The Shanghai Special District Local Court issued an official letter stating: "The association's letter requested a detailed explanation of the actual procedure for handling the application for a protest certificate and the simple methods that the holder and the court should use, so that it can be forwarded to the members for their reference. The court should be applied with a written statement, and the original of the rejected negotiable instrument should be attached to the statement. The stamp duty should be purchased and affixed in accordance with the Provisional Rules for Fee Collection for Non-Contentious Matters. The receiving and dispatching office of this court will receive the statement and notify the applicant to wait for processing. The statement will then be sent to the division for handling. This method is as agile as other non-contentious matters. (3) The Shanghai Local Court issued an official letter stating, "The association's official letter and the official letter of the Special District Local Court, which attached an oil-printed order and a sample protest certificate, have been received. The holder of a negotiable instrument is to apply to the court for a protest certificate. The application should be made with a written statement, and the original of the rejected negotiable instrument should be attached and delivered immediately. Fees should be paid in accordance with non-contentious matters. Unless there are special circumstances, the applicant can wait in court for processing in accordance with the law without having to wait for approval in order to expedite the process."

He successively defrauded the Xin Sheng Chang, Tong Ju Long, and Yi Shun Chang customs brokerages on Jixiang Street of a total of five hundred yuan in foreign currency before fleeing. Later, the heads of the three brokerages inquired with Detective Zhang and learned they had been deceived. News from Trade Associations

▲ Tobacco Exchange Industry: The Shanghai South Office of the Tobacco Exchange Trade Association issued a notice yesterday regarding the deadline for registration for the unified match tax: "We recently received a letter from the Great China Match Company stating that they had inquired about the deadline for tax exemption on match inventories and all related procedures, which have been fully noted. After investigation, match inventories that have been inspected and certified by the Unified Tax Bureau are limited to be sold and cleared by February 15th and may still be subject to customs duties according to past practices. After this deadline, the unified tax will be levied according to regulations. The procedures for inspection and verification during the sales period are summarized as follows: (1) All matches cleared through customs from February 1st to February 16th, if the box surface is affixed with a inventory inspection certificate and holds a inventory ex-factory certificate, is considered as proof, and is exempt from the unified tax within the deadline. inventory customs shall collect customs duties in accordance with regulations. (2) If the company has a match tax payment certificate issued by the Ministry of Finance Unified Tax Administration or an export tax exemption permit, it is considered as goods that have paid the unified tax, and customs should stop collecting customs duties. (3) If there is no match inventory certificate, tax exemption certificate, or tax exemption certificate within the deadline, please instruct the customs to first go to the unified tax district bureau or the nearest unified tax resident customs office in each province to pay the unified tax according to regulations without collecting customs duties. (4) The above items shall be replied to by letter, and I hope that you will check and inform all members of your association.

▲ Envelope Industry: The Envelope Industry Association held a general meeting for the election of executive committee members at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. Thirty-seven members signed in. Member Wei Zhuohua was publicly elected as temporary chairman. After performing the formalities, the chairman delivered the opening speech and announced the procedures for the ballot election. The elected executive committee members were Wei Huanghua, Chen Hengyun, Xu Jinfu, Zhao Zhengxi, Xia Rongsheng, Guo Yingyong, Wu Tongfu, Yu Xiaodi, and Ji Baoer. The alternate members were Gui Jinlong, Li Kunfu, and Wang Xizi. After the election, the elected members mutually elected Wei Zhuohua as chairman of the committee and head of the general affairs department. Chen Henglian and Xu Jinfu, Zhao Zhengxi as standing committee members, Chen Henglian as standing committee members for the accounting department, Wu Tongfu and Xia Rongsheng as members of the supervision group, Guo Yingyong, Li Baoer as members of the investigation group, and Yu Xiaodi was in charge of general affairs. The meeting adjourned late, and the date of the inaugural meeting will be announced to the public at the inauguration to show seriousness.

▲ Restaurant Industry: The Restaurant Industry Association held its 12th executive committee meeting on February 11th. Chairman Cheng Kefan reported the incoming letters. Matters for discussion: (A) Regarding the payment of association fees and public debt funds to the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, it was resolved to pay according to the amount of capital. (B) Regarding the collection of funds for the tax regulations research association of various trade associations, it was resolved to subsidize 5 yuan in foreign currency. (C) Requesting opinions on the business tax regulations of various industries and reference to all regulations and bylaws promulgated, it was found that the restaurant industry is taxed at 20 per mille of business according to Jiangsu regulations. It was decided to send a letter to the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce requesting the government to reduce the collection to a maximum limit of 2 per mille, and that both the Chinese and French Concessions should be held at the same time. (D) The Municipal General Chamber of Commerce's letter attached the association's articles of association was resolved to be filed for future reference. (E) The outline of the business tax collection method shall be implemented in accordance with the method to be decided upon after reduction. (F) The Trademark Law promulgated by the Ministry of Industry and the forty articles of the proposed detailed rules were resolved to be filed for future reference, others were omitted. The meeting adjourned.

Local News Two

Robbery and Murder of a Bandit on Catholic Church Street Last Night

▲ Bodyguard Opens Fire and Hits a Bandit

▲ Four Robbers, One Dead, Three Escaped

At 7:05 last night, four robbers suddenly appeared at the Chengfeng Woolen Goods Store, No. 9-10 Xiangyu Lane, Catholic Church Street, French Concession, plotting a robbery. Fortunately, the bodyguard of the store was vigilant and ambushed behind the banister. When the robbers went upstairs, he suddenly opened fire. As a result, one robber was shot twice and fled out the door, collapsing on the way. The details are recorded below:

▲ Opening a Woolen and Knitting Goods Store for Eight Years Mr. Hu, a native of Ningbo, has been operating the Chengfeng Woolen and Knitting Goods Store at No. 9-10, Alley 1, Xiangyu Lane, Catholic Church Street, French Concession for eight years. The remaining rooms are rented to Longzhang Indigo Store, Chengzhi Pigment Store, Hengji Photographic Film Material Store, and Yijuxing Woolen and Sundries Store. The main door of No. 10 has been closed for years, and entry and exit are through the main door of No. 9.

▲ Hiring a Bodyguard for Defense To avoid being targeted by bandits, Mr. Hu hired a bodyguard a year ago for security, as there are many stores in the building and the location is quiet. The bodyguard, named Wu Jingui, is from Shandong, nearly 30 years old, exceptionally strong, and particularly vigilant. Hu valued him highly and specifically purchased a self-defense pistol to prevent emergencies.

▲ Four Robbers Arrive Suddenly, Two with Handguns At 7:05 last night, four robbers arrived, two wearing blue cloth robes, one wearing a gray serge gown, and one wearing a purple sauce-colored silk robe, covered with an old overcoat. They spoke with a northern accent. Two robbers were armed with handguns and rushed in through the main door. At that time, Hu's driver, A-Xi, was about to go out to urinate and encountered the robbers face to face. The robbers had already detected that Hu had hired a bodyguard. Upon seeing A-Xi, they mistook him for the bodyguard.

▲ Bodyguard Vigilantly Ambushes in the Dark Upon seeing A-Shan, the robbers immediately held the gun against A-Xi's chest, forbidding him from making a sound. One robber held a gun to watch him. The three robbers went straight into the parlor. However, the bodyguard Wu Jingui was standing idly in the parlor and saw several people rushing in, taking out a gun to scare A-Xi. Knowing that he had encountered a robbery, he quickly retreated behind the screen, took out his self-defense pistol, loaded the bullet, and hid in the darkness behind the stairs, waiting in ambush.

▲ One Robber Shouts, and the Bandits Flee One robber was responsible for watching the driver and also acted as a lookout. The remaining robbers entered the hall, looking around, appearing very flustered, and repeatedly shouting, "Where is the money? Get it out quickly!" After shouting, they walked towards the screen, intending to go straight upstairs. However, just as he reached the middle section of the stairs, two gunshots suddenly rang out. At the same time, a robber wearing an overcoat cried out, "Ah yo, ah yo" repeatedly. Seeing that the situation was not good, the robbers quickly turned around and fled out the door.

▲ The Wounded Bandit Falls and Dies It turned out that the two gunshots were fired by the bodyguard. One robber had been shot twice and, wounded, fled out of the alley, went south to Avenue Edward VII, turned west, and then went north into Zhubao San Road. However, the wounded robber had just fled to the entrance of No. 29 when he fell to the ground and died due to injuries to vital parts. The remaining robbers took the opportunity to escape without a trace. The patrolman from post No. 289 saw him, sent him to Renji Hospital nearby by car. After the doctor's examination, it was found that he had already died. He immediately notified the police station, which sent detectives to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall to examine the body.

▲ The Dead Bandit Had Two Bullets in His Body The examination revealed that the dead bandit had two bullets in his body. One hit his abdomen, going in from the front and out from the back, and the other pierced his right chest and right shoulder. The bandit had a slightly pockmarked face, was about 30 years old, wore an old overcoat, a dark sauce-colored silk robe, silk pants, his hair was combed back, black silk socks, velvet shoes, and wore a black copper basin hat. The body is waiting for an autopsy this afternoon.

Organization of the Gongfa Company

▲ Two Accountants Cleared Yesterday

▲ Stating That There Is No Partnership or Agreement

▲ Accountants Reported to the Social Bureau Yesterday

Accountants Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang previously inquired about the partnership agreement and shareholder list of Gongfa Company. They received a letter from the company yesterday, but it was not formally stamped. They immediately replied, "Replying directly, we have received your company's reply of February 11th, stating that you inquired about the Gongfa Company's partnership agreement and shareholder list. The situation is difficult for outsiders to understand, because Gongfa Company is not a partnership and has no agreement. Now, we will give a simple answer in good faith, hoping for your understanding. Ten years ago, Mr. Huang Chujiu initiated the night market exchange at the Great World, starting with rapid success and great prosperity. Later, due to the exchange turmoil, he was caught in a vortex, leading to failure. Mr. Huang felt quite uneasy about the suffering shareholders, so he merged the established Great World Day and Night Bank, Chinese and Western Pharmacy, Fuchang Tobacco Company, and Hot Spring Bathhouse into one, reorganizing it into Gongfa Company. He converted the shares of the night market exchange, etc., at a discounted price of 50% for each share of ten yuan, into a total of 700,000 yuan (Huang accounted for about 60%) as shares of Gongfa Company. He solemnly declared to the shareholders that he would do his best to ensure that all shareholders recovered their losses. Since then, Mr. Huang has been fully responsible in the capacity of chairman and general manager. Although interest has never been interrupted, dividends have never been distributed. Shareholders' meetings and board meetings have not been held for several years, making it difficult to comply with the company's regulations. In short, we trusted them too much, leading to today's results, which is very painful. The above is all the truth. We hope for your understanding. The incoming letter is responsible for replying in the name of Gongfa Company, but it is not stamped (with the Gongfa Company seal, it is difficult to use as a formal letter. Accordingly, we reply to your company and request that you quickly stamp it formally. Accountants Wu and Pan submitted to the Social Bureau yesterday, saying, "Submitting directly, we previously received Decree No. 6323 from your bureau, instructing our accountants to submit the articles of association and the list of shareholders and directors of Gongfa Company to the bureau as soon as possible, and to report the liquidation situation at any time. We have already submitted a report on receiving and keeping the Shanghai Day and Night Bank and the Shanghai Great World Savings Department (i.e., the Savings Department) and the balance sheet for inspection on February 2nd. Now, we will copy the abridged plan for the liquidation of the bank and department and the handling situation ordered by the French Concession Mixed Court to your bureau for your inspection and filing. Furthermore, our accountants were appointed as liquidators of the bank and department by the French Concession Mixed Court on February 9th. In addition to the published announcement, we jointly present this to the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau.

The High Court Still Needs to Inquire in Detail About the Dalun Real Estate Lawsuit

▲ The Municipal General Chamber of Commerce Replied to the High Court

▲ Various Key Points Are Still Not Clear

The Great China Department Store previously leased a piece of land near Zhifu Lane on Nanjing Road from Dalun Real Estate Company to demolish and build a seven-story department store. Because the existing tenants refused to move, they were in litigation with Dalun Real Estate Company, preventing the Great China from starting construction. Although the Great China purchased the land from Dalun, the tenants refused to move because the transfer of ownership should be restricted while the lawsuit was in progress. Since Dalun disagreed with the second-instance judgment and appealed to the Supreme Court, the court reviewed the files and believed that there were doubts about the second-instance judgment. The court sent it back to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court for retrial last month. The High Court followed the instructions of the Supreme Court and sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal General Chamber of Commerce to investigate. It is recently reported that the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce has now replied to the High Court truthfully. Regarding the point of whether there is any custom for not signing a lease contract during the investigation, it said that there is no precedent to cite. As for the economic flow and commercial prosperity after the opening of the Great China Department Store, it must depend on the situation of the company's operation in the future, and it is impossible to predict it now. Although the High Court has received a reply, it is still unclear. It plans to subpoena both parties to court in the near future for detailed questioning.

Female Student Demands Divorce

▲ Both Lawsuits Were Rejected

▲ Plans to Appeal to the Supreme Court Again

▲ Accusing Wife of Non-Virginity on Wedding Night

▲ Maid Recounts the Young Madam's Suffering

Ms. Zhai Xiuying, a student at the Patriotic Girls' School, is 29 years old and quite beautiful. She married Shen Rongzong last year. Shen is 27 years old and studied at Fudan University. The couple suddenly divorced after only a few months of marriage. Xiuying claimed that she could not bear Shen's abuse, so she filed a petition with the Special District Local Court a few days ago, requesting a divorce. The court rejected it. Zhai was still unwilling to give up and entrusted lawyers Lu Qi and Wu Shou Gong to appeal to the Second Branch of the Higher Court. On the afternoon of the 4th of this month, the first hearing was held. The hearing was conducted by Judge Hu Yigu of the Second Civil Court. Because both parties were in academia, many male and female students attended the court that day, and most of them were classmates of both parties. Yesterday was the date of the verdict. The previous trial situation and the verdict are recorded as follows:

▲ Previous Trial Situation After Judge Hu took the seat, the plaintiff Zhai Xiuying shyly stated the reasons for the divorce, saying that there were two points: (1) She could not bear her husband's abuse. Before the marriage, both parties did not want to get married. It was all based on the orders of her parents and the words of the matchmaker. On the wedding date, Shen avoided marriage in Hangzhou. Within a few months of marriage, she was beaten three times. From this point of view, what is the normal affection between husband and wife? (2) She suffered serious insult from her husband. On the wedding night, he accused me of not being a virgin. One day, I accompanied my sister to the New World at my mother's request, and he accused me of going to a brothel, slandering me completely. Under such circumstances, it is really difficult to grow old together. She should be allowed to divorce. After stating this, Judge Hu ordered the witness, the maid A-Xiu, to the witness stand, asking how the relationship between the Xiuying couple was usually. A-Xiu replied that the young madam and the young master had a bad relationship. When she returned home after a full month, the young master searched the young madam's handbag repeatedly. The young master really didn't treat the young madam like family members, guarding against her like a thief. Moreover, the young master did not sleep in the same bed with the young madam at night. After the young madam went to the New World, she was slapped twice, punched once, and kicked once when she returned, and the next day, blood was found in the spittoon. At this point, Judge Hu questioned Shen Rongzong again. Shen confessed that he had studied at Fudan University. The marriage was decided by both parents and obtained my consent. Before marriage, the two parties communicated and were deeply in love. After marriage, they were also deeply affectionate. This divorce lawsuit is not Xiuying's intention, but her father's claim. Judge Hu immediately ordered the lawyers of both parties to begin the debate. After the lawyers of both parties debated each other, Judge Hu announced the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict for the afternoon of the 11th of this month.

▲ Yesterday's Due Date for Verdict Yesterday, Judge Hu still opened the civil court to pronounce the verdict. Zhai Xiuying did not arrive, and Shen Rongzong arrived on time to await the verdict. The appeal was immediately dismissed. It is heard that Zhai Xiuying is still unwilling to accept it and plans to appeal to the Supreme Court again.

Husband and Wife Eat Puffer Fish and Die Together

▲ One Fish Kills Two Lives

Jin Liangshi, a woman from Jiangbei, was 45 years old and used to collect wild vegetables everywhere. She bought a puffer fish at the market the day before yesterday, brought it home for cooking, and ate it with her husband Kui Guangsheng. At first, they felt the taste was exceptionally delicious, but three hours later, their abdomens gradually became painful due to the swelling of the fish roe. They cried for help. Neighbors hired a car to send them to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The hospital did not keep female patients, so Jin Liangshi was changed to Guangren Hospital, but both were beyond salvation. They both died at 8:00 PM. The police received the report and sent detectives to the Fielun Road to examine the bodies. Prosecutor Guo from the Special District Local Court was commissioned to the office for examination, ascended to the public seat, and questioned the deceased's nephew Jin Wenxi and his friend Qin Cunyu, who surrendered to claim the body. After approval, Jin and others made a statement and took it away for burial.

Frank Buck Left Shanghai Yesterday

▲ The Grand Meeting at the Cathay Hotel Yesterday

▲ Du Xigui Specially Gave Several Embroidered Items

American movie star Frank Buck arrived in Shanghai the night before last. Yesterday morning, he and the World Tour Group took cars to tour the streets.

About 100 people participated, mostly foreigners. On the Chinese side, those who attended included Admiral Du Xigui, Zhao Jinqing, Director of the Industrial and Commercial Delegation, Wu Jingxiong, former President of the Provisional Court, Diao Minqian, Director of the Information Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Liu Yunfang, Deputy Director of the Foreign Affairs Office, and Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai University. The Accuser in the Xin Xin Employee Embezzlement Case Sentenced to Six Months in Prison

▲ Zhou Shuqing Commits the Crime of Joint Embezzlement

▲ Given Probation for Two Years Due to Surrender

Zhang Shiying, Weng Hengqi, Yang Fuyuan, and others, retired employees of Xin Xin Company, colluded and embezzled more than 180,000 in account funds when they were employed years ago. They were exposed recently, and Inspector Wang Changgeng detained them and sent them to the Special District Local Court for separate punishment, which has been reported in this newspaper. It is found that a total of 13 people participated in the embezzlement. Zhou Shuqing, who reported this time, was also a member of the embezzlement group and is still working at the company. The director of the company, thinking that he had surrendered, did not pursue the matter generously, so he was not sued jointly with Zhang Shiying and others. However, the Legal Group of the Bureau of Public Works believes that the law cannot be selectively applied. Since Zhou jointly embezzled, he should be held criminally responsible. Although he surrendered, the law has provisions for cases of surrender. It seems insufficient to warn those who commit fraud if they want to completely avoid criminal liability by surrendering. Therefore, he still sued Zhou for joint embezzlement in the Special Court. Zhou admitted that it was undeniable that he jointly embezzled. Judge Zhou sentenced him to six months in prison for the crime, and announced a two-year probation in court, considering that he surrendered.

Verdict on the Russian's Opening of a Casino

▲ Defendants Sentenced to Two Months Imprisonment and Fined

▲ Plaintiff Countersued for False Accusation, Sentenced to One Month Imprisonment

Gao Laisi Re Gao Fu, the president of the Russian Military Society at No. 9 Tongfu Road, accused Ai Hai Ying Peng Fan Che Lin in the Special District Court of three crimes: seizing the society, opening a casino, and intimidating with a gun. The case had been heard several times, and the details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday was the date for the verdict. At 2 PM, Judge Cheng Shangfeng opened the Fifth Court to pronounce the judgment. The plaintiff, defendants, and their respective lawyers were all present on time to await the verdict. After Judge Cheng took the bench, the lawyers from both sides first engaged in a round of debate. Judge Cheng then asked the plaintiff and defendants a few questions before declaring the debate in this case closed and awaiting the verdict. The main text of the judgment is as follows: Ai Hai Ying Peng Fan Che Lin are each sentenced to two months imprisonment and a concurrent fine of 400 yuan in silver for the crime of jointly providing a place for gambling with the intention of making a profit. The other charges are acquitted. Gao Laisi Re Gao Fu is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of false accusation, which is reduced in penalty. The number of days of detention before the judgment becomes final can be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. If the fine cannot be paid, it can be commuted to imprisonment at a rate of three yuan per day. During the appeal period, the defendants are allowed to be released on bail of 2,000 yuan, and the defendant Gao Laisi Re Gao Fu in the countersuit is allowed to be released on bail of 400 yuan.

Pirates Outside Wusong Estuary Request Amnesty

After the various pirate gangs outside the Wusong Estuary engaged in infighting, they attacked each other on the sea, resulting in mutual slaughter. Xia Jingeng and Wife's Divorce Case

▲ Both Parties to Go Out and Reconcile Again

Xia Yao, the wife of Xia Jingeng, filed a criminal lawsuit in the Special District Court, through lawyer Shi Lin, against her husband for the crimes of assault and abandonment, seeking a divorce. Judge Cheng Shangfeng had previously heard the case once and ordered the parties to reconcile outside of court and rescheduled the hearing, as reported in previous newspapers. Because the reconciliation between the two parties failed, Judge Cheng opened the Fifth Court again yesterday afternoon at 2 PM to hear the case. After briefly questioning both parties, he declared that since they are husband and wife and have lived together for eight years and have children, reconciliation without divorce is the best solution. According to the court's opinion, Xia Yao should return home with her husband immediately, and Xia Jingeng should issue a statement promising to give Xia Yao 20 yuan in silver each month for living expenses, so that they would not need to litigate again to avoid suffering. When asked if Xia Jingeng agreed, Xia answered in the affirmative. When asked if Xia Yao agreed, Xia Yao replied that 20 yuan per month was not enough and that she had no guarantee. Judge Cheng said that you should return home with your husband, and Xia Jingeng will issue a statement promising to give you 20 yuan per month. If he does not give you the money, you can still sue him. If you want more, I don't think Xia has the ability to provide it. He further instructed that, whether you agree or not, the court must handle the case in this way. Xia Yao then replied, "In that case, he has a mistress. Can the court rule for a divorce?" Judge Cheng said that this was another issue, but at the same time, he instructed Xia Jingeng, "You should not abandon your wife and have an affair with someone else." Xia replied that he did not have a mistress. At this point, Shi Lin, the plaintiff's lawyer, stood up and requested the court to reschedule the hearing to allow for another reconciliation. Judge Cheng agreed, saying that whether you agree or not, reconciliation is best; otherwise, the verdict will be pronounced next time.

Fire on Huakang Road Kills an Apprentice

The Tang Yin Ji Laundry, located at No. 15 and 16 Huakang Road, Zhabei, was a double-fronted store owned by Tang Shunsheng. At around 2 AM yesterday morning, while the people in the store were sound asleep, a fire suddenly broke out in the kitchen downstairs due to carelessness. In an instant, the three rooms and two side rooms were completely destroyed. Before long, the fire spread to the neighboring Baohua Silk Weaving Factory, which was also burned to the ground. Xu Yongzhang, an apprentice at Tang Yin Ji, was unable to escape in time and perished in the fire. Fire trucks arrived and tried their best to put out the fire, which was finally extinguished after an hour. Tang Shunsheng, the owner of Tang Yin Ji, was arrested by the Fourth District Police Department and taken for questioning. It was found that he had fire insurance of 3,000 taels. He was ordered to be sent to the bureau for investigation. The apprentice who died in the fire was 11 years old and from Fenghua.

County Government Bans Bird Guns

The Shanghai County Government believes that privately owned bird guns can easily be used by criminals as murder weapons, which is detrimental to public security. It is imperative to strictly ban them in accordance with the Hunting Law and its Implementation Rules to curb the source of chaos and maintain local peace. Yesterday, it instructed the district chiefs to comply with the ban and report back at any time. (Huadong News Agency)

Two men froze to death in Nanshi and Zhabei the night before last. One was found in Xingren Lane outside the 16th Pier in Nanshi. He was a man in his twenties, wearing an old Yuan cloth uniform and checkered cloth pants. The other was found in Jiuan Lane, Jiaotong Road, Zhabei. News from the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Association Regarding Shaanxi

The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Association received a message from Shaanxi yesterday, stating that the province has suffered from successive years of disasters, and the people are in dire straits and in urgent need of relief. Now that it is the severe winter season, with ice and snow on the ground, and the time when the old harvest is gone and the new harvest has not yet come, the disaster victims are freezing and starving, on the verge of death. Winter relief is now extremely urgent. The provincial relief association is actively preparing according to plan, such as distributing cotton clothes, setting up shelters, and opening porridge kitchens, of which there are more than 20. It is striving to provide relief. Recently, the porridge kitchens have reported that the disaster situation in various places is still very severe, and the disaster victims are waiting for relief like expecting clouds and rain, but the amount of food is too small and the number of tickets is limited, making it difficult not only to help the masses but also to maintain the current situation. They are presenting petitions to the provincial relief association, requesting that porridge be allocated to maintain the porridge kitchens, as the situation is as precarious as a pile of eggs. To save the survivors of this disaster and give them a chance to live, if food and money are not available, then there may be no survivors left.

Passenger Dies Before Boarding Ship

Yesterday afternoon at around 6 PM, a man, about 30 years old and appearing to be a worker, carrying a suitcase and an umbrella, bought a ticket at the Ningshao Pier on the 16th Pier, intending to board the Ningshao steamer to Ningbo. At that time, the ticket seller noticed that the man's face was pale and his breath was weak, as if he was seriously ill. Fearing that something might happen after he boarded the ship, he ordered the No. 1 patrolman of the Ningshao Company to escort him to the Red Cross Hospital in Nanshi for treatment. Unexpectedly, the man died shortly after arriving at the hospital, before he could be treated. The company then reported the matter to the First District Police Department for investigation. As the case involved a human life, the 16th Pier Jia (local head) was ordered to report it to the Shanghai Local Court for an autopsy.

Dutch Steamer Boatswain Dies from Coal Gas Poisoning

There was a Dutch steamer at buoy No. 31 and 32 in Yangshupu, which employed two Dutchmen as chief steward and second steward. The night before last, the weather turned suddenly cold, and it snowed heavily. The two men burned coal in the cabin to keep warm and were both poisoned by coal gas. The chief steward died immediately, while the second steward suffered severe coal gas poisoning and was sent to the hospital for treatment. The deceased was examined and collected by a medical officer from the Customs Health Department.

News of the Italian Lending Bank

▲ Dividends Still at Eight Percent

News from the local China-Italy Bank stated that it had received a telegram from the Italian Lending Bank, stating that the bank's board of directors had completed the audit of last year's accounts and would convene a shareholders' meeting to report on the results and request the payment of an 8% dividend. The bank's dividends have been 8% in previous years, but it is rare to achieve this result in the current depressed economy. This is because the bank's operations are proceeding step by step, and the plan approved at last year's meeting has been fully implemented, which is why the board of directors is very satisfied.

Initiation of the Chaoshan Plum Blossom Viewing Event

Seven miles south of Tangqi Town in Hangzhou, there are two mountains, Chaoshan and Mashan. Chaoshan is in the south, and Mashan is in the north. The twin peaks are verdant and reflect each other north and south. In this beautiful spring season, the red and green plum blossoms of Chaoshan and the cherry blossoms and peonies of Yunshu Pavilion on Mashan are fragrant and colorful, making them well-known scenic spots. In order to introduce the famous scenic spots of Hangzhou and encourage the interest of men and women in spring outings, the Hangzhou China Travel Service has specially organized a Chaoshan Plum Blossom Viewing Event. The round-trip travel fee is only 4 yuan per person. The date is set for February 22nd (postponed if it rains). At 8:30 AM, gather at the China Travel Service on Hubin Road in Hangzhou. At 9:00 AM, depart from Hangzhou by car. Around 9:00 AM, you can reach Chaoshan. The travel service will send a special person to take care of you, visit the Daming Hall and Zhong Sheng Temple, admire the plum blossoms at the top of Lion Peak, and then visit the famous scenic spots such as Dayuan Temple, Maming Temple, Anyin Temple, and Yunshu Pavilion on Mashan. Then take the original car back to Hangzhou.

Women's Association to Hold Tea Dance Party

▲ Xu Zi Provides Subsidies for Charity

The Chinese Women's Association (formerly the Shanghai Women's Association) is scheduled to hold a tea dance party at the Dahua Hotel on February 27th, Friday, starting at 9 PM, with the proceeds from the tickets used to subsidize free schools and local charities. This kind of gathering is held once a year and has been uninterrupted for 12 years. The schools established by the association are located on Chide Road and Caojiadu, respectively, with a total of more than 100 poor children (boys and girls) enrolled. In addition, a school is established in the Qiu Jiang Road Children's Universal Benefit Society, specializing in enrolling students who have been rescued from the Northwest famine provinces. A school is established on Luo Sheng Road to facilitate women's after-work study. Now that the funds have been raised, two more free schools will be opened in Yangshupu and West Hongqiao to benefit women. In addition to providing free education, the association also donates to the Chinese Red Cross and provides relief to the Northwest famine, etc. The newly elected officers of the association this year are: President Mrs. Ma, Vice President Mrs. Ling Xianyang and Mrs. Xia Peng, Treasurer Mrs. Huang Hanliang, Secretary Mrs. Jiang, Document Clerk Mrs. Lin Jiao, Public Relations Mrs. Wen Yuqing, Board Member of Free School Miss Yang Xizhen, Honorary Advisor Mrs. Mei Huaquan.

Gasoline Prices Increased Yesterday

Due to the further decline in silver prices, major coal companies in this city increased the prices of gasoline and motor oil yesterday (11th). Currently, the wholesale price of the best motor oil is 1.25 yuan per gallon, and the ordinary gasoline is 1.225 yuan per gallon. In the future, the best motor oil will be sold for 12.9 yuan per two cans of five gallons each, and gasoline will be sold for 12.6 yuan. The current price of aviation gasoline is 14.1 yuan per case, the best motor oil is 11.3 yuan per case, and ordinary gasoline is 11.05 yuan per case.

Since taking office, Tao Xianqu, director of the First Precinct of the Fifth District of the Zhabei Public Security Bureau of Shanghai, has strictly enforced security and prevention in his jurisdiction, and the merchants and residents deeply appreciate him. Director Tao took the initiative to mediate and resolved the issue peacefully. "Love and Blood" Opens in Paris Today

John Gilbert and Joan Crawford are both well-known big stars in the film industry. Their artistic excellence has long been recognized, but they have never worked together before. Not long ago, the two stars collaborated on a film called "Love and Blood," set against the backdrop of the romantic hell of New York City, USA. It focuses on depicting the magic of women and the greatness of love, making people feel deeply moved and captivated. According to American media reviews, the film's success is comparable to the previous collaborations between Gilbert and Ms. Garbo. It is reported that the film will be released today at the Paris Grand Theater on Avenue Joffre.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin and the coastal area south of Ma'anshan are cloudy and cold with rain and snow. The Shandong coast is sunny. There are northeasterly winds in the Yellow Sea and the East China Sea. Education News · Important News

Boy Scout Registration Regulations

▲ Boy Scout Headquarters Has Revised and Promulgated Them for Compliance

The Boy Scout Headquarters of China issued a directive to all troops yesterday, stating: "In order to ensure compliance, the Chinese Boy Scout Troop Registration Regulations have been revised and are hereby promulgated. A copy of the revised Chinese Boy Scout Troop Registration Regulations is attached. Please ensure that your troop complies with them." Here is the original text of the regulations:

Article 1: Any Chinese Boy Scout Troop organized in accordance with the Chinese Boy Scout Troop Organization Regulations must complete registration in accordance with these regulations. Article 2: Matters regarding the registration of Chinese Boy Scout Troops shall be handled by the county and city councils and submitted to the Headquarters for review at each level. Article 3: In counties and cities where councils have not been established, the registration matters in the preceding article shall be handled by the provincial council and submitted to the Headquarters for review. Provinces and cities where councils have not been established may submit directly to the Headquarters for handling. Article 4: Chinese Boy Scout Troops requesting registration must fill out three copies of the registration form. The registration form will be determined separately by the Headquarters. Article 5: Chinese Boy Scouts requesting registration must pay a registration fee of 4 yuan in national currency. Article 6: After the Chinese Boy Scout Troop Headquarters reviews and approves the registration, the Headquarters will assign a troop number and issue certificates, flags, seals, etc. Article 7: If any of the following circumstances are discovered after a Chinese Boy Scout Troop has been registered, the Headquarters will revoke its registration: 1. Having speech or actions that violate the Three Principles of the People; 2. Having fewer than 18 registered members; 3. The troop leader has left office and there is no successor; 4. Not complying with the laws and regulations of the Chinese Boy Scouts. Article 8: The Chinese Boy Scout Troop Registration Certificate is valid for one year. After the expiration, it must be re-registered. Article 9: The registration period for Chinese Boy Scout Troops shall be determined by the Headquarters. Article 10: These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented by the Boy Scout Headquarters of China.

Qingpu Education Bureau Pays Attention to Promoting the Gregorian Calendar

The Qingpu County Education Bureau is sparing no effort in promoting the Gregorian calendar. On December 29th of last year, it was discussed at the principals' meeting, and it was unanimously advocated that all schools in the county should do their best to promote it. The bureau also resolved at the ninth bureau affairs meeting to have all bureau members set out during the Lunar New Year holiday to inspect educational institutions in each school district. It is reported that the inspection personnel have been internally determined, with the General Affairs Section for the first district, the Social Education Section for the second district, the Director for the fourth district, the Supervisors for the seventh and eighth districts, and the education committees for the remaining districts separately responsible. It is scheduled to depart on February 14th and 15th, lasting about a week, and at least one-half of the schools must be inspected. The bureau also resolved at the ninth bureau affairs meeting to issue a notice to all schools in the county to establish literacy centers to assist in the promotion of civil education.

Local

City Education Bureau Reissues Order Prohibiting Teachers and Students from Taking Leave

▲ From February 10th to the End of February

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Order Shang Zi No. 175 to all schools in the city (no separate documents): "It is hereby ordered that the municipal government has previously issued the Measures for Promoting the Gregorian Calendar New Year, which this bureau has already copied and forwarded in Directive No. 2366 for compliance, and should be strictly enforced. Article 7 of the measures stipulates, 'Teachers and students are prohibited from taking leave from February 10th to the end of February unless they are ill or have important matters; violations will be punished.' Teachers and students are not allowed to take leave without reason during this period. It goes without saying that schools should hold classes as usual during this period, and should not suspend classes at will except on Sundays. In order to prevent this from happening, this order is hereby reiterated. All schools in the city must comply with it and not violate it." February 11, 1931, Director Xu Peihuang.

City Education Bureau Orders High Schools to Report Entrance Qualifications for New and Transfer Students

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Order to Municipal High Schools and Registered Private High Schools: "It has been stipulated that the entrance qualifications for new and transfer students in secondary schools should have been stipulated long ago, but it is common to see cases of forging certificates and skipping grades, which is wrong. Starting from the second semester of the 19th year, each school should submit the entrance qualifications of the new and transfer students admitted, along with the grade applied for, together with the graduation certificates and transfer certificates, to this bureau for verification. A list of forms is attached for your school to follow."

City Education Bureau Orders High Schools to Report Course Credit Hour Schedules and Teaching Materials

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Order to Municipal High Schools and Registered Private High Schools: "The Ministry of Education has stipulated provisional standards for many important courses in junior and senior high schools, which this bureau has already forwarded for implementation. It has been found that the courses in each school vary greatly, and often increase or decrease at will without following the Ministry's regulations, which is inappropriate. In order to correct this, your school must comply with the Ministry's standards and make corrections starting from the second semester of the 19th year. You must also submit the course credit hour distribution schedule, the teaching material schedule, and the daily schedule for each grade to this bureau for verification within one week of receiving this document. The teaching material survey form is distributed with this order, and the other two forms should be determined by the school itself."

Ministry of Education Orders Reorganization of Peking University and Normal University

Women's Normal College to Merge with Normal University

Russian College of Law and Politics No Longer Enrolling New Students

All Colleges and Institutes to Set Up Preparatory Courses and High Schools to Run an Affiliated High School

The Ministry of Education has ordered the reorganization of Peking University, the Russian College of Law and Politics, and Peking Normal University. The orders are listed below:

(1) Order to Peking University Wen

"It is found that the existing organization of Peking University is mostly the result of factual succession. The system is complex and difficult to manage thoroughly. Teaching equipment and management in all aspects are gradually declining. It is difficult to improve the efficiency of education without making changes and reorganizing. The following measures are hereby stipulated regarding the organizational aspects of the university that should be improved:

(1) The Women's Normal College and its affiliated schools will no longer be subordinate to Peking University starting this semester and will merge with the original National Peking Normal University to form the National Peking Normal University, temporarily divided into the First Department and the Second Department. (2) The central government has formulated other measures to cultivate Russian specialists. The Russian College of Law and Politics, originally subordinate to Peking University, should be gradually closed down starting this year and will no longer enroll new students. A closing committee should be established, organized by three members selected and hired by the president of Peking University, to handle the closing and preside over the college affairs. During the closing period, it will still be temporarily called the Russian College of Law and Politics and will be subordinate to Peking University, but no new president will be appointed. (3) The existing departments and classes of the Law School will remain as they are for the time being. How to change the subjects or run other colleges starting next school year should be carefully investigated by Peking University and a plan should be submitted to the Ministry for approval. (4) The College of Art should be closed down in accordance with the previous order of the Ministry. Peking University is responsible for supervising and reorganizing the college affairs and saving costs. (5) The Women's College should be renamed the Women's College of Arts and Sciences starting this semester to match its name and reality, and efforts should be made to enrich its content. If it is necessary to increase funding, Peking University should make overall arrangements and supplement it from the college's funding scope and submit it to the Ministry for approval. (6) The organization of the President's Office of Peking University should be appropriately expanded in order to effectively reorganize school affairs. The president of Peking University should formulate an organizational outline and submit it for approval. The expenses increased due to the expansion should not exceed 2,000 yuan per month and should be planned and subsidized by Peking University from the funds of each college and submitted to the Ministry for approval. (7) The preparatory courses and high school classes set up in the colleges and institutes of Peking University should be planned in detail by Peking University to jointly run a perfect affiliated high school. Peking University should implement the above measures to seek improvement and report the implementation to the Ministry for record."

(2) Another Order to Peking University Wen

"Yesterday, the Ministry of Education ordered Peking University to resolve the turmoil in the Russian College of Law and Politics, approving the resignation of President Duan Qitang and dismissing the teachers and staff involved in the turmoil, stating: 'It has been found that the student unrest in the Russian College of Law and Politics of the university has been prolonged, and the dispute has become increasingly serious. The Ministry has ordered Xie Shuying, Section Chief, to go to investigate and report on the abandonment of college affairs and the students' blocking of accounting and other excessive actions, which is very distressing. It is reported that the president of the college, Duan Qitang, has applied for resignation and should be approved immediately. All accounts of the college should be checked and submitted by the president to the university for detailed review and reported to the Ministry for record. The teachers and staff of the college who were involved in the turmoil and have been dismissed should not be rehired. In addition to the fact that the college should be closed down year by year, the Ministry has separately ordered the university to comply and take responsibility for supervising and reorganizing."

(III) Order to Beiping Normal University

It has been decided by the Ministry that the Women's Normal College and its affiliated schools, originally under the jurisdiction of Beiping University, will no longer be under the jurisdiction of Beiping University from this semester. They will be combined with the university to form the National Beiping Normal University, to create a perfect institution in the country for training secondary school teachers and educational administrators, and for researching educational academia. At a time when the nation is rectifying education, the school bears a very heavy mission. The following are the matters that need to be improved urgently in the university:

(1) The National Beiping Normal University after the merger will be temporarily divided into two parts, the first and the second. The departments and classes of the original National Beiping Normal University will be the first part, and the original Women's Normal College will be the second part. The principal of National Beiping Normal University shall draft detailed measures on how to avoid duplication of the departments set up in the two parts, and how to unify the organization and establish colleges in accordance with the University Organization Law to gradually abolish the separation of the two parts, and submit them to the Ministry for approval before the summer vacation of this year. (2) After the merger, the funds of the Women's Normal College and its affiliated schools will still be distributed according to the original allocation, and the Normal University will receive them all at once. The expenditure of the funds will remain the same as before this year, but efforts must be made to be thrifty. The principal of National Beiping Normal University shall draft detailed measures on how to plan and redistribute the funds as a whole in the next year, and submit them to the Ministry for approval. (3) The Normal University should focus on cultivating secondary school teachers and educational administrators, and on researching educational academia. After the merger, the university's curriculum, equipment, training, etc., should be based on this purpose, and should be stipulated separately. The affiliated primary and secondary schools and kindergartens must be fully utilized to give normal students more opportunities for practical training. (4) All the affiliated primary and secondary schools and Montessori kindergartens of the original Beiping Normal University and Women's Normal College will be temporarily operated as before, but they should be gradually planned to become an integrated affiliated school of the Normal University in the future, and there should be a close connection between the university and the affiliated school, so that the main functions of both parties can be gradually completed. The above items should be earnestly implemented by the university to seek improvement. This order is hereby issued for compliance, and the handling situation should be reported for reference. This order.

Thirteen people, including Ting Xu Peihuang, Yu Hongjun, and Hou Dachun, were present. Pan Gongzhan chaired the meeting, and Pan Runsheng recorded the minutes. The meeting was held as usual. The chairman reported. Xu Peihuang, Pan Gongzhan, and Wu Kaixian were elected as executive committee members by ballot, and many other important cases were discussed and decided. The meeting adjourned.

Dr. Hua Xuming Arrives in Shanghai Tomorrow

▲ The Characteristics of the Winnetka System

The American educator Dr. Carleton W. Washburne will come to China on the 13th of this month to give lectures. Few people in the country know much about the doctor's life. According to him, the doctor is a researcher of individual education, the creator of the so-called "Winnetka System." He graduated from Stanford University and has been engaged in elementary school education for many years. He deeply suspected the school class system and was determined to study individual teaching. He initially started to try it out, but was repeatedly opposed by the educational authorities. In 1919, Dr. Hua Xuming was hired by a small school in Winnetka Town near Chicago to conduct a large-scale individual education experiment. The characteristics of the experiment are briefly described below:

1. The Winnetka system contains four important principles: (1) to enable children to obtain as much knowledge and skills as possible that can be applied to their future lives; (2) to enable each child to naturally, happily, and perfectly enjoy their childhood life; (3) the progress of mankind lies in the full development of each member; (4) the welfare of the people must be in the development of the entire social translation of each member.

2. The curriculum of the Winnetka system includes two parts: (1) a part of the course includes knowledge and skills that are sufficient to cultivate children's socialized attitudes; (2) a part of the course includes stimuli and environment that are sufficient to cultivate children's efforts in creative work.

3. The individual teaching implemented by the Winnetka system includes three special processes: (1) the goal of the curriculum is determined according to the needs of society and is organized with reference to the children's ability to develop in each period; (2) the compilation of teaching materials can enable children to learn by themselves and correct their own mistakes; (3) the image of Sir Hua Xuming, the creator of the Winnetka system

The compilation of diagnostic tests can be adapted to the application of each stage of learning. 4. The Winnetka system completely breaks the class teaching. In the Winnetka school, there is no distinction between grades. A certain child must sit in a certain classroom, and all are distinguished by social age. The so-called "social age" refers to the fact that he can be most united with other children in the classroom.

5. The Winnetka system pays special attention to group and creation activities. The activity center is mostly concentrated in social science or literature. The purpose is to stimulate children to discover their personality, inspire their instincts and creativity, cultivate their sense of service, and their awareness of the welfare of the masses, in order to save the malformed development of individual education.

6. In the classrooms of Winnetka schools, there is no recitation or explanation. Diagnostic tests are used instead of recitation. On the other hand, there are more group and creative activities. Because there are children's self-study materials, there is very little need for teachers to explain.

Regarding the details of Winnetka, it is heard that the Children's Education Society, a domestic organization specializing in the study of children's education, will publish a special issue of Winnetka in the journal "Children's Education," which will be published by Kaiming Bookstore soon.

Their result was unfortunately defeated in the final with Italy to win the European zone final.
